    Method for Preparing Five-Color Galls for Black Hair

    Select larger five-color galls, remove any insect debris, and crush them into small pieces.

    First, divide them into coarse and fine portions. Place the coarse pieces in a ceramic vessel and roast them over low heat until they form a paste. Then add the fine pieces and continue roasting. At first, dark smoke will rise; keep stirring without stopping. Once cooled, reheat and roast again until yellow smoke appears, then remove from heat and stir. Heat once more until blue-green smoke starts to emit, then stop heating.

    Take a large piece of true blue cloth, dampen it, and squeeze the five-color galls onto the cloth to form a ball, then press it into a cake with your foot. Cover with a load of wet mud and let it set overnight; the ideal color should resemble that of crow feathers. Do not allow any air to escape from the ceramic vessel.

    Easy and Simple Recipe for Black Hair Dye

    Use one qian (a traditional weight unit) of five-color galls, 0.4 grams of salt, 0.2 grams of elm bark powder, and 0.7 grams each of copper sulfate and white alum. Grind all ingredients into fine powder, mix with tea until it becomes like thin porridge, and let it thicken in hot water. Apply while still warm in the evening; it can blacken hair for a month.[30p]

    Preparation for Hair Dyeing and Treatment

    Gold lead: one penny
    Blue powder: three parts
    Sea sand: one part
    Camphor: half part

    Mix the above ingredients evenly, and use them to apply to the beard and hair with tea infusion. After waiting for a stick of incense to burn out, wash it off and apply oil to nourish.

    Point White Formula
    Cinnabar: one and five-tenths parts
    Silver ore: three pennies
    Angelica: three pennies
    Alum: one part
    Fly powder: one part
    Genuine powder: one part

    Mix these ingredients with clean water to remove white hair, then use a silver hairpin to dot at the root of the hair, causing new growth to be black.

    Soaking Oil to Remove White Hair
    Silver ore: one tael
    Angelica: three taels
    Walnut oil: eight taels

    Grind these three ingredients into powder and soak them in a ceramic jar for seven days before applying.

    Black Cloud Powder
    Five-fold gall: roasted
    Various herbs: boiled
    Fresh walnut skin
    Green pomegranate skin
    Haritaki fruit
    Green papaya skin
    Green persimmon skin
    Roasted soapwort
    Bird's nest grass
    Green vitriol
    Asarum
    Mercury: equal parts

    Take mercury and insert it into pomegranate skin, leave it for over a month, then dry the pomegranate skin, grind it with the other herbs into powder and form into pills the size of small coins. Regularly roast in charcoal ash without leaving the fire. If you want to use this for feathered hair, first wash it with soapwort water, then use hot wine to dissolve and apply, vinegar can also be used.

    Nourishing Powder (from "Charming Bamboo Hall Formula")

    Ginseng: one tael

    Jiawei Cangzhu Gao
    With prolonged use, the essence becomes abundant, energy strong, hair turns from white to black, and teeth fall out then grow again.
    Take ten jin of Cangzhu, pound it to a paste, place it in a large pot, add two buckets of water, and boil with gentle and vigorous heat until reduced to over ten bowls. Strain the liquid through silk, and place it in a ceramic jar.
    Add four liang each of ginseng, raw and cooked Rehmannia, Huangbai, Yuanzhi, Duzhong, Chuanxiong, walnut meat, Chuanjiao, broken ancient paper, and angelica prepared with ginger; two liang of Qingyan; one liang of Zhush, two bowls of dried lotus grass juice; and two jin of white honey. Grind these medicines into powder, mix them into the Cangzhu paste, seal it tightly, and boil in a large pot of water with two incense sticks as a measure. After seven days buried in the ground, take two to three spoonfuls each time, mixing with wine soup as desired, twice daily, to nourish essence, energy, and spirit.

    Yizui Bulao Dan
    This specifically nourishes blood, turning gray hair to black.
    Take two liang each of lotus flower pistils, raw Rehmannia, and Huai jiaozi, Wujia pi; and six stones of Mo Shi.
    Pound the above ingredients using a wooden stone mortar, place in a clean silk bag, combine with ten jin of fine clear wine, and put in a clean jar, sealing it tightly. Soak in spring and winter for one month, autumn for twenty days, and summer for ten days. After soaking for the required days, consume as desired, drinking until intoxicated. Must continue to take daily until the wine is finished; if hair remains white, it will turn black. If it does not, repeat the preparation; taking it will yield the desired effect.[35p]

    　　中山还童酒 【《回春》，下同】 　歌曰：中山还童酒，人间处处有。善缘得遇者，便是蓬莱叟。　　马蔺子一升，埋土中三日　马蔺根洗切，一升　　右用黄米二斗，水煮成糜，陈曲二块为末，酒酵子二碗，并前马蔺子共和一处做酒，待熟；另用马蔺子根一升，用水煮十沸，入酒内三日。每月搅匀去滓，随量饮醉。其酒饮尽，须发尽黑。其酒之色，如漆之黑。
    　　经验乌须酒　能变白为黑，身轻体健，功不可述。　　大枸杞二升，要每年冬十月壬癸日，面东采摘红肥者，捣破　　右用好无灰酒二斗，　同盛于磁器内，浸二十一日足，开封，添生地黄汁三升搅匀，各以纸三层封其口，俱至立春前三十日开瓶，空心暖饮一杯，至立春后髭须都黑。勿食三白。[36p]

    Zhongshan Rejuvenation Wine

    The song goes: "Zhongshan Rejuvenation Wine, available everywhere in the world. Those with good fate and encounters are the immortal elders of Penglai."

    Take one sheng of bluebell root, bury it in the ground for three days. Clean and chop the bluebell roots, one sheng.

    Now use two dou of yellow millet, boil it into a paste, and take two pieces of aged wine yeast to grind into powder, along with two bowls of wine yeast. Combine all the ingredients, including the bluebell roots, and make the wine, waiting for it to mature. Additionally, take another sheng of bluebell root, boil it in water ten times, then add it to the wine for three days. Stir and remove the dregs each month, drinking as desired to achieve intoxication. Once the wine is finished, hair and beard will turn entirely black. The color of this wine is as black as lacquer.

    Experience has shown that the black mustache wine can transform white to black, making one light and healthy; its efficacy cannot be fully described.

    Take two sheng of goji berries, picking the ripe and plump ones facing east on the day of Ren and Gui in the tenth lunar month each year, and crush them.

    Next, take two dou of good non-ash wine, mix it in a ceramic vessel, and steep for twenty-one days. After opening, add three sheng of fresh rehmannia juice, mix well, and seal the mouth with three layers of paper. Open the bottles thirty days before the arrival of Spring, drink one cup warm on an empty stomach, and thereafter, all hair will turn black after the arrival of Spring. Avoid eating anything white.[36p]

    Chrysanthemum Powder: Treats yellow and dry hair, making it black and lustrous. Ingredients: chrysanthemum, cornelian cherry fruit, leaves of arborvitae, ligusticum, angelica, asarum, mulberry bark, and roots, flowers, and leaves of dry lotus, each one tael. Grind and mix, for every two taels, add three bowls of water, decoct until reduced to two bowls, strain, and wash the hair to make it black.

    Wuyun Powder: Treats yellow and white hair that lacks luster. Ingredients: copper sulfate, cinchona, decoction of various herbs, papaya skin, myrobalan peel, sour pomegranate peel, green walnut skin, pig’s tooth soap, fo-ti, and asarum, in equal parts. Grind to a fine powder, mix with honey into coins-sized pills, and store in charred ash, ensuring it does not leave the ash. When using, dissolve in hot wine for application.

    Erxian Pills: Treats hair loss effectively. Ingredients: dried leaves of arborvitae, eight taels; whole angelica, four taels. Grind without iron tools into powder, mix with water to form pills the size of walnuts. Take five to seventy pills daily, twice.

    Shengtu Wuyun Oil: Promotes new hair growth. Ingredients: Sichuan pepper, angelica, and ligusticum, each one tael; cornelian cherry fruit, cinnamon, and aconite, each five qian. Grind coarsely, place in a silk bag, and soak in one and a half jin of scented oil for twenty-one days. Afterward, take the oil to rub on the scalp to promote new hair growth.[37p]

    　　五倍子不拘多少，捶碎去灰，入砂锅内炒，烟尽为度，以青布打湿扭干裹之，脚踏成饼为末，每用钱半　乌黑霜即炒黄好细面，四两　当归尾一两，为末　白芨末，一两，三味搅匀，每用一分半　红铜末，不拘多少，火内烧极红，投入水碗中，取出再烧，再投，取水内自然之末，用水淘净，酢煎数沸，至干，随炒黑色，每用一分半　明白矾末，一分半　青盐一分二厘　没石子二厘半　诃子肉二厘半，二味俱用面包，入砂锅内，将桑炭同拌，炒至焦干　　右为末，以浓茶调匀，以酒盏盛贮，用铁杓注水，煮如糊，先将皂角水洗净须发，然后涂药包裹一夜，次早洗去，以胡桃油涂之，令润。[38p]

    Secret prescription for dark hair: Crush and remove ash from gall nuts without measuring how much, stir-fry in a sand pot until smoke dissipates. Wrap in damp blue cloth and step on to make crumbs. Use 0.5qian at a time. For black frost, stir-fry until it turns a fine yellow, four liang. One liang of Chinese angelica root, as fine powder. One liang of whitening powder, combine these three. Use 1.5fen at a time.

    Red copper powder in any amount, burn until red hot and transfer into a bowl of water, then remove and burn again, process until natural powder is left. Clean with water, boil in vinegar until dry, then stir-fry until blackened, using 1.5fen at a time.

    Mix 1.5fen of alum powder, 1.5fen of blue salt, 2.5liang of vitex fruit, and 2.5liang of chebule fruit, both ground to flour, in a sand pot with mulberry char and stir-fry until crispy.

    This mixture should be combined with strong tea, stored in a wine cup, and using an iron ladle, mix with water until it reaches a paste. First, wash the hair with soap water, then apply the medicine and wrap it overnight. Wash off in the morning and apply walnut oil to keep it moisturized.[38p]

    External Dyeing with Black Cloud Ointment
    To prepare, take two pieces of stones, roast them until yellow, incorporate with copper powder, add one and a half qian each of white alum and white salt, and five qian of gallnut. Grind these into a fine powder. Mix this powder with strong tea to make a uniform paste. Boil in water until it turns black. Use as directed, and the hair will turn black.

    Shenxian Liuzi Pill: For men over thirty, taking this medicine, one year with two single doses will prevent graying and keep hair black. Ingredients: Tu Si Zi prepared, Jin Ling Zi, Fu Pen Zi, Wu Wei Zi, Gou Qi Zi, and She Chuang Zi, all 1 liang; He Shou Wu soaked in wine and roasted; Niu Xi soaked in wine and roasted; Di Gu Pi and Shu Di Huang soaked in wine, each 3 liang; Bo He and Chuan Mu Guo, each 2 liang.     Lead Comb [From "Pujifang"]
    Bird whiskers.
    Ten taels of lead, three taels of tin, magnet, soap alum, myrobalan skin, stone powder, pomegranate skin, sulfur, and black sesame oil, each two and a half qian; raw and cooked rehmannia, and needle sand, each half a tael; three mulberries; one tael each of madder root and walnut skin.
    Grind these into a powder. First melt the lead and tin, mix in half of the powder with willow wood, pour into the comb mold, and imprint to shape the teeth. Boil the remaining powder with water for three days and nights, adding water as needed. Take it out, wrap in cloth, and let it sit for five days. Each time, use cooked leather to cushion and comb one hundred strokes. First, cleanse with soap pod water and wipe dry.

    Xiongxin Decoction treats the above conditions.

    Prepared Aconite, peeled and with the navel removed; raw Aconite; Tian Nansheng; fried Licorice; dried Ginger; Chuanxiong; and Fragrant Cyperus in equal parts. Grind and take four qian, with five slices of ginger and a little bud tea, and decoct.

    Qingzhou White Pills treat the above conditions.

    Large Pinellia processed; clean White Aconite, lightly roasted; Gastrodia; whole Scorpion; slightly roasted Chuanwu, with the skin and tip removed; and cleaned Tian Nansheng, lightly roasted, all in equal parts. Grind into a fine powder, use fresh ginger juice to make a dough, form into pills the size of Wutong seeds. Take ten pills initially, gradually increasing to twenty pills, using tea or warm water after meals.

    Internal use of Black Hair Pills is suitable for those whose hair turns white from excessive bleeding.

    Fetal hair and blue salt, each four taels, placed in a sealed jar, roasted with incense three times until cool. After cooling, grind into a powder. Prepared He Shou Wu, nine times steamed and dried Wintergreen seeds, drought lily grass, Angelica, Goji berries, fresh Rehmannia, and Poria, each four taels; one tael of Ginseng. Use ten bowls of water, boil down to five bowls of liquid. Then, remove the dregs, concentrate into a paste, mix in the powdered fetal hair and blue salt, and divide into several small jars. When taking, dissolve three to five teaspoons in boiling water or wine.[42p]

    Xionggui Neituo San
    For treating tiger must toxicity.
    Ingredients: Chuanxiong, Danggui, Chenpi, Bai Fuling, Tianhuafen, Jiegeng, Yinhua, Huangqi each 10 grams; Licorice 5 grams; Water 2 cups, decoct down to 80% and take after meals.

    Neishu Huanglian Tang
    For treating the above symptoms.
    Ingredients: Muxiang, Huanglian, Shanzhizi, Danggui, Huangqin, Baishao, Bohe, Binglang, Jiegeng, Lianqiao each 10 grams; Licorice 5 grams; Dahuang 20 grams; Water 2 cups, decoct down to 80% and take before meals. Adding 2 teaspoons of honey is also acceptable.

    Ruyijinhuang San
    For treating the above symptoms.
    Ingredients: 10 jin of flower pollen, Huangbo, Dahuang, Jianghuang each 5 jin; Houpu, Chenpi, Licorice, Cangzhu, Naxing each 3 jin; Baizhi 3 jin. Grind to fine powder, mix with tea and honey for application.

    Jingfang Baidu San
    For treating the above symptoms.
    Ingredients: Jinge Sui, Fangfeng, Qianghuo, Duhuo, Qianhu, Chaihu, Chuanxiong, Jiegeng, Fuling, Zhihua each 10 grams; Sheng Licorice, Ren Shen each 5 grams; 3 slices of ginger; Water 2 cups, decoct down to 80% and take on an empty stomach. If very cold, add 3 stalks of scallion.

    Simple Prescription[44p]

    　　染白发令黑：取针砂二钱，酢浸七日，取出晒干，炒黑，入没石子一个，为末，搽之即黑。【《本草》，下同】
    　　地黄干熟二种，皆黑须发良药，丸服或酿酒服之，并佳。
    　　发白：用牛膝煎服，或酿酒服之佳。
    　　发落不生：以酢泔洗净，布揩令热，以腊猪脂入生铁煮，三沸涂之，便生。 【《千金翼》】
    　　眉发落不生：先用生姜擦三次，后用半夏生为末，麻油调涂之即生。 【《入门》】
    　　男女粘发，或因油膏而粘滞者，取竹沥涂之即解，和炒盐尤妙。 【《野语》】
    　　何首乌：黑须发，末服、丸服，或酿酒服皆佳。 【《本草》】
    　　妇人发落：芭蕉油涂之，长发令黑。
    　　槐实久服，令须发不白。

    　　黑桑椹变白发，酿酒服之佳。又取一斤和蝌蚪一升，瓶盛封口，悬屋东头，百日尽化为黑泥，染白发髭，黑如漆。
    　　母丁香以生姜汁研，拔去白发须，涂孔中，即生黑者矣。又白蜜涂孔中，亦生黑者。[45p]

    Dyeing white hair back to black: Take two qian of needle sand, soak it in vinegar for seven days, remove it, dry it in the sun, fry it until black, add a stone to it, grind it into powder, and apply it to restore blackness.

    Both dry and mature rehmannia are good medicines for black hair; they can be taken in pill form or brewed in wine, which is also excellent.

    For white hair: Boil and take cow knee, or brew it in wine for better results.

    For hair loss with no regrowth: Wash thoroughly with vinegar, wipe with cloth until hot, boil with lard from a young pig in cast iron until three boils, and apply it; this will promote hair growth.

    For loss of eyebrow hair: First, rub with fresh ginger three times, then grind half summer (Pinellia ternata) into powder and mix with sesame oil for application to encourage regrowth.

    For sticky hair in men and women, possibly due to oil or pomade: Applying bamboo juice will relieve it, especially when mixed with fried salt, which works wonderfully.

    He Shou Wu (Fo-tso): Good for black hair; can be taken as powder, in pill form, or brewed in wine.

    For women experiencing hair loss: Apply banana oil to make the long hair black.

    Taking sophora fruit over a long period will prevent beard and hair from turning white.

    Black mulberry can turn white hair black when consumed in wine. Additionally, take one pound mixed with one liter of tadpoles, seal in a jar, and suspend it at the east of the house; it will transform into black mud in a hundred days for dyeing white hair and beard to black as lacquer.

    Mother clove ground with ginger juice can pull out white hairs; apply it to the root, and it will turn black. Applying white honey to the root can yield a similar result.[45p]

    　　胡桃外青皮和蝌蚪为泥，染白须令黑；又胡桃仁取油涂须发，令黑润有光。
    　　胡麻生取油涂头，生秃发；又乌麻九蒸九晒为末，枣膏丸服，令白发还黑；又取叶煎汤，沐头长发。
    　　蔓菁子压取油涂头，能变蒜发。

    　　头痒，生白秃疮，发落：取熊脂常常涂之，令人生发长且黑。
    　　发落：熊脑髓作油涂之。

    　　头发黄赤：生柏叶末一升，猪脂一斤，和丸弹子大，每以布裹一丸，纳泔汁中，化开沐之，一月色黑而润矣。【《圣惠方》】
    　　发落：羊粪烧灰，淋汁沐头，令易生而黑；又须发落，羊粪和雁膏傅三宿，即生。 【《本草》，下同】
    　　发落：取腊月猪鬐膏火上烊化涂之，即生。发薄不生亦宜。
    　　染须方：用蚰蜒四十条，以京墨水养之三日，埋马矢中，一月取出，以白丝头试之，如即黑到尾；再入马矢中埋七日，再取试之，性缓，乃以捻须，庶不致黑皮肤也。【《普济方》】[46p]

    Walnut green skin and tadpoles mixed with mud can dye white hair black; also, walnut kernels can be used to extract oil to apply to hair, making it black, moisturized, and shiny.
    Black sesame oil applied to the head can prevent baldness; furthermore, black sesame can be processed—steamed and sun-dried nine times into a powder—then combined with jujube paste into pills to restore white hair to black; additionally, leaves can be brewed to wash hair and promote growth.
    Rapeseed oil, extracted from crushing seeds, can change white hair to black.

    For itchy scalp leading to white sores and hair loss: regularly apply bear fat to promote hair growth and keep it long and black.
    For hair loss: bear brain marrow, made into oil, should be applied.

    For yellow or red hair: mix one sheng of crushed cedar leaves and one jin of pig lard, form into balls the size of a marble, wrap each ball in cloth, and immerse in fermented liquid; after it dissolves, wash with it. In one month, the hair will be black and shiny.
    For hair loss: burning sheep dung ash and rinsing the head with its juice encourages hair regrowth and keeps it black; also, for hair loss, mixing sheep dung with wild goose fat and applying it for three nights will promote hair growth.
    For hair loss: melting fat from the back of a pig in the twelfth lunar month and applying it will stimulate regrowth. For thinning hair that does not grow, this is also suitable.
    For dyeing facial hair: use forty centipedes, soak them in ink for three days, bury them in horse dung for a month, then test with a white silk to see if it has dyed; if so, bury again for seven days in horse dung, check again for gentleness, then twist the hair so as to avoid blackening the skin.[46p]

    　　病后发落：猢狲姜、野蔷薇嫩枝煎汁刷之。
    　　揩齿变白发方：酸石榴皮一个，泥裹，烧令通赤，候冷去泥，用茄子根与槐枝同烧，令烟绝，急以器盖之，候冷；用槐枝，马齿苋墙上生者好，不令人见，采；薄荷、石膏、五倍子烧熟、川升麻各一两为末，揩牙不但变白为黑，亦且坚牙，甚妙。
    　　拔白生黑良日：正月四日，二月八日，三月十三，四月十六，五月二十，六月二十，七月二十八，八月十九，九月二十五，十月一日，十一月十一日，十二月十日，早起拔之，永不白。又正月五日、十三日，二月八日、十八日，三月三日，四月十三、二十五，五月五日、十五日，六月十四、二十四，七月十八、二十八，八月九日、十日，九月八日、十八日，十月十三、二十三，十一月十日，十二月十六日。已上月日，并用午时前拔之。凡拔时，先以水于石上磨丁香汁，候拔了，急手敷于毛孔中，即生黑者。[47p]

    After recovering from an illness: boil the tender branches of wild roses and monkey ginger to make a juice for application.

    To make teeth turn from white to black: take the skin of one sour pomegranate, wrap it in clay, and burn it until it turns red; let it cool and remove the clay. Burn eggplant roots along with locust branches until the smoke ceases, then cover immediately and wait for it to cool. Use locust branches from the wall where purslane grows, and harvest them unseen. Grind one tael each of mint, gypsum, and gall nuts until fine, then use this mixture to clean your teeth. Not only will they turn from white to black, but also become stronger—truly remarkable.

    Favorable days to turn white hair black: the 4th of the 1st month, 8th of the 2nd month, 13th of the 3rd month, 16th of the 4th month, 20th of the 5th month, 20th of the 6th month, 28th of the 7th month, 19th of the 8th month, 25th of the 9th month, 1st of the 10th month, 11th of the 11th month, and 10th of the 12th month. Rise early on these days to pluck, and it will never go white. Additionally, the 5th and 13th of the 1st month, the 8th and 18th of the 2nd month, the 3rd of the 3rd month, the 13th and 25th of the 4th month, the 5th and 15th of the 5th month, the 14th and 24th of the 6th month, the 18th and 28th of the 7th month, the 9th and 10th of the 8th month, the 8th and 18th of the 9th month, the 13th and 23rd of the 10th month, the 10th of the 11th month, and the 16th of the 12th month. On these dates as well, pluck in the morning hours. When plucking, first grind clove juice on a stone with water; immediately after plucking, quickly apply it to the hair follicles to encourage them to turn black.[47p]

    　　变白方：取老生姜刮皮一大升于铛中，以文武火煎之，不得令过沸其铛，惟得多油腻者尤佳。更不须洗刮，便以姜皮置铛中，密封固济，勿令通气，令一精细人守之，地色未分时，便须煎之，缓缓不得令火急。如其人稍疲，即换人看火，一伏时即成，置磁钵中，研极细。虽曰一伏时，若火候匀，至日西即药成也。使时以小簪脚蘸取如麻子大，先于白发下点药讫，然后拔之；再点，以手指热捻之，令入肉，第四日当有黑者生，神效。【《李卿方》】[48p]

    To make the whitening remedy: Take one large sheng jiang (fresh ginger) and scrape off the skin, placing it in a pot. Use gentle heat to simmer, ensuring the pot does not boil over, and it is best if the ginger is very oily. There is no need to wash or scrape further; simply place the ginger skin in the pot, sealing it tightly to prevent air from entering. Have a careful person monitor it. When the color has not begun to separate, you must begin to simmer it without letting the fire get too hot. If the person monitoring feels fatigued, they should switch places with someone else. The mixture will be ready after one hour of simmering and should be placed in a clay bowl and ground finely. Although it says an hour, if the heat is even, it can be ready by sunset. When using, take a small amount on the tip of a fine stick, about the size of a sesame seed, and first apply it to the white hairs, then remove it; afterwards, apply again, using a warm finger to massage it into the skin. By the fourth day, some black hairs should start to appear, demonstrating its remarkable effectiveness.[48p]

    　　人无发：取甜瓜叶捣汁涂之，即生。
    　　发落不生，令长：用麻子一升，熬令黑，压油，以敷头发上。
    　　长发方：麻叶、桑叶二味，以泔煮，沐发七次，可长六尺。 【《千金方》】
    　　乌须明目：用黑铅半斤，锅内溶汁，旋入桑条灰，柳木搅成沙，筛末，每早揩齿，以水漱口洗目，能固齿明目黑须发。【《胜金方》】
    　　揩牙乌髭：用黑铅消化，以不蛀皂荚寸切投入，炒成炭，入盐少许，研匀，日用揩牙。摘去白髭，黑者更不白也。　　又方：黑锡一斤，炒灰，埋地中五日，入升麻、细辛、诃子同炒黑，日用揩牙，百日效。【《普济方》】[49p]

    • For hair loss: Take sweet melon leaves, crush them to extract the juice, and apply it; it will regenerate.
    • If hair has fallen and you want it to grow: Use one liter of sesame seeds, roast them until black, press out the oil, and apply it on the hair.
    • To promote long hair: Combine two ingredients, hemp leaves and mulberry leaves, and boil them in clean water; wash your hair seven times for a potential growth of six feet.
    • For darkening hair and improving eyesight: Use half a pound of black lead, dissolve it in a pot, mix in ash from mulberry twigs and grind with willow wood into a fine powder; each morning, clean your teeth with it, rinse your mouth, and treat your eyes. This can solidify teeth and darken hair.
    • For darkening teeth and mustaches: Use black lead processed; cut non-cavitated soap pods into small pieces, roast them into charcoal, mix in a little salt, and grind it well to use daily for tooth cleaning. White hairs will diminish, and the black ones will not turn white.
    • Another remedy: Take one pound of black tin, roast it into ash, bury it in the ground for five days, then mix and roast it with embelia, asarum, and myrobalan, and use it to clean your teeth daily; effects will be visible in a hundred days.[49p]

    　　令发长黑：用熊脂、蔓荆子为末等分，和匀酢调涂之。 【《圣惠方》】
    　　赤秃发落：香油、水等分，以银钗搅和，日日擦之，发生乃止。 【《普济方》，下同】
    　　白秃无发：麻子炒焦研末，猪脂和涂研末，猪脂和涂，发生为度。
    　　发落不生：蕡麻子汁煮粥，频食之。 【《圣济总录》】
    　　头发不生：侧柏叶阴干作末，和麻油涂之。 【《梅师方》】
    　　染白须发：胡粉、石灰等分，水和染之，以油纸包，烘令温暖，候未燥，开，洗去，以油润之，黑如漆也。【《博物志》】
    　　染白须发：用针砂酢炒七次一两，诃子、白芨各四钱，百药煎六钱，绿矾二钱，为末，用酢热调刷须发，菜叶包住，次早酸浆洗去。此不坏须，亦不作红。　　又方：用针砂、荞面各一两，百药煎为末，茶调，夜涂旦洗；再以诃子五钱，没石子酢炒一个，百药煎少许，水和涂一夜，温浆洗去，黑而且光。[50p]

    • For promoting long black hair: Use bear grease and viburnum fruit, ground evenly, mixed with vinegar for application.

    • For red baldness: Mix sesame oil and water in equal parts, stir with a silver needle, and apply daily until hair growth resumes.

    • For white baldness: Roast and grind sesame seeds, mix with pig fat for application until hair growth is achieved.

    • For hair loss without regrowth: Boil ramie seed juice into porridge and consume frequently.

    • For hair not growing at all: Dry side cedar leaves in the shade, powder them, and mix with sesame oil for application.

    • To dye white beard hair: Mix equal parts of talc and lime, add water to dye, wrap in oiled paper, heat until warm, then, when not dry, open and wash off, lubricate with oil for a color as black as lacquer.

    • For dyeing white beard hair: Use one ounce of ground iron sand and stir-fry it seven times in vinegar, add four qian each of chebula fruit and white lily, six qian of various herbs, and two qian of green vitriol to make a powder. Mix with hot vinegar to brush on the beard and cover with vegetable leaves, then wash off with sour liquid the next morning. This method does not damage hair and does not turn red.

    • Another method: Use one ounce each of ground iron sand and buckwheat flour, powder with boiled medicinal herbs; mix with tea for application at night, wash in the morning. Also take five qian of chebula fruit, fry with a little stone vinegar, and mix a small amount of boiled herbs and water for overnight application; wash with warm liquid to achieve black and shiny results.[50p]

    　　发落不止，乃肺有劳热，瘙痒：用石灰三升，水拌炒焦，酒三升浸之，每服三合，常令酒气相接，则新发更生，神验。【《千金方》】
    　　染发乌须：矿灰一两，水化开，七日，用鉛粉一两研匀，好酢调搽，油纸包一夜。先以皂角水洗净，乃用。【《集元方》】
    　　涂染白发：绿矾、薄荷、乌头等分为末，以铁浆水浸，日染之。 【《相感志》】
    　　发须黄赤：生地黄一斤，生姜半斤，各洗，研自然汁，留滓；用不蛀皂角十条，去皮弦蘸汁，炙至汁尽为度。同滓入罐内，泥固，煅存性，为末。用铁器盛末三钱，汤调，停二日。临卧刷染须发上，即黑。【《本事方》】[51p]

    1. For persistent hair loss due to lung heat and itching: Use three sheng of lime, mix with water, fry until charred, and soak in three sheng of wine. Take three he each time, making sure the wine fumes are prominent, resulting in new hair growth with effective results.

    2. For dyeing hair black: Dissolve one tael of mineral ash in water for seven days. Mix with one tael of lead powder, adjust with vinegar, and apply. Wrap with oil paper overnight. First, wash thoroughly with soapwort water, then use.

    3. For dyeing white hair: Take equal amounts of green vitriol, mint, and monkshood, and grind them into powder. Soak in iron water for daily dyeing.

    4. For yellow or red hair: Take one jin of fresh rehmannia and half a jin of fresh ginger, wash, and grind to extract the natural juice, leaving the dregs. Use ten pieces of non-decayed soapwort, peel and treat with the juice, roasting until the juice is exhausted. Combine the dregs in a jar, pack tightly, and calcine for preservation into powder. Use three qian of the powder, mix with soup, and let it sit for two days. Apply before sleeping by brushing onto hair and beard for a black color.[51p]

    　　金陵煎，益须发，变白为黑。金陵草一秤，六月以后收采，拣青嫩无泥土者，不用洗，摘去黄叶捣烂，新布绞取汁，以纱绢滤过，入通油器钵盛之，日中煎，五日；又取生姜一斤，绞汁，白蜜一斤合和，日中煎，以柳木篦搅勿停手，待如稀饧，药乃成矣。每月早及午后各服一匙，以温酒一盏化下。如欲作丸，日中再煎，令可丸，大如梧桐子，每服三十丸。及时多合为佳，其效甚速。【《千金月令方》】
    　　乌须固齿：七月取旱莲草连根一斤，用无灰酒洗净，青盐四两腌三宿，同汁入油锅中，炒存性，研末，日用擦牙连津咽之。　　又方：旱莲草取汁，同盐炼干，研末擦牙。 【《摄生妙用方》】　　又方：旱莲草一两半，麻枯饼三两，升麻、青盐各三两半，诃子连核二十个，皂角三挺，月蚕沙二两，为末，薄酢面糊丸弹子大，晒干，入泥瓶中，火煨，令烟出，存性，取出研末，日用擦牙。【《奉亲养老书》】[52p]

    Golden Nanjing Essence, particularly effective for hair, transforms white to black. One pound of Nanjing grass, harvested after June, should be selected for its tender and clean leaves, without any dirt. No washing is required; remove the yellow leaves and crush the remainder. Extract the juice using new cloth and filter it through fine silk into an oil-infused vessel, boiling it at noon for five days. Additionally, take one pound of fresh ginger, extract its juice, and combine it with one pound of white honey, boiling this mixture again at noon. Stir continuously with a willow stick until it reaches the consistency of a thin syrup; the medicine will then be complete. Each month, consume a spoonful in the morning and another in the afternoon, dissolving it in one cup of warm wine. If you wish to form pills, boil it again at noon until suitable for shaping, each pill should be the size of a Paulownia seed, and take thirty pills each time. It is better to take them in larger quantities as their effect is very swift.

    For blackening teeth: In July, take one pound of dry lotus grass with roots, wash it with ash-free wine, and pickle it with four ounces of blue salt for three nights. Combine the juice in an oil pot and fry until well done, then grind it into a powder to be used for brushing teeth and swallowing the saliva daily.

    Another method: Take the juice from dry lotus grass, mix it with salt, and dry it. Grind into powder for brushing teeth.

    Yet another recipe: Take one and a half ounces of dry lotus grass, three ounces of hemp cake, three and a half ounces each of dodder and blue salt, twenty whole myrobalan seeds, three sticks of soap pod, and two ounces of silkworm sand, grind them into a powder. Make small balls the size of pellets with thin vinegar dough, dry them, place them in a clay bottle, and heat over fire to release smoke. Store carefully, then grind into powder for daily use for brushing teeth.[52p]

    　　发黄不黑：蓖麻子仁香油煎焦，去滓，三日后频刷之。 【《摘元方》】
    　　坚齿乌发：大(艹舌)蒌一个，开顶，入青盐二两、杏仁去皮尖三七粒，原顶合扎定，蚯蚓泥和盐固济，炭火煅存性，研末，每日揩牙三次，令热，百日有验。如先有白须拔去以药投之，即生黑者。其治口齿之功，未易具陈也。【《普济方》】
    　　染乌髭发：干瓦松一斤半，生麻油二斤，同煎，令焦为末，另以生麻油浸涂，甚妙。 【《圣济录》，下同】
    　　少年发白：土马鬃、石马鬃、五倍子、半夏各一两，生姜二两，胡桃十个，胆矾半两，为末，捣作一块，每以绢袋盛一弹子大，用热酒入少许浸汁，洗发一月，神效妙极。
    　　染发令乌：酢煮黑大豆，去豆煎稠染之。 【《千金方》】[53p]

    Yellow but not black: Fry castor bean oil until charred, strain, and brush frequently after three days.

    For firm teeth and black hair: Take one large wild loofah, cut the top, add 200 grams of blue salt and 37 peeled bitter almonds, secure the top, mix with earthworm clay and salt, fire and calcine, then grind to powder. Brush your teeth three times a day until warm for a hundred days to see effect. If there are white hairs, remove them and apply the medicine to turn them black. The efficacy in treating teeth is not easy to elaborate.

    For dyeing gray beard and hair: Use 750 grams of dry pine needles and 1000 grams of raw sesame oil, boil until charred and grind to powder, then apply again with sesame oil for excellent results.

    For youthful white hair: Use 30 grams of soil horsehair, horsehair stone, sumac, and half summer, 60 grams of ginger, ten walnuts, and 15 grams of blue vitriol, grind to a paste, form into balls each in a silk bag, soak in hot wine for a month, yielding miraculous results.

    For dyeing hair black: Boil black soybeans, remove the beans and boil the residue to thicken for dyeing.[53p]

    　　揩牙乌须：麻枯饼八两，盐花三两，用生地黄十斤取汁，同入铛中熬干，以铁盖覆之，盐泥泥之，煅赤，取研末，日用三次。揩毕即饮姜茶，先从眉起，一月皆黑也。【《养老书》】
    　　染须方：大乌龟一个，饿一二日，将饭与肉骨果子烟火之食饲之，三五月后，夜间以漆盒盛之，用竹片置盒口，令通气，外放灯一盏，盒内热，龟自撒尿；急则以麻油烟熏鼻，亦即尿。先用五倍子末炒酢如胶，若尿得一小锺，入五倍酢半锺，入磁器炆一滚即止，牛角罐收贮，以新笔略蘸搽须，多用面黑。
    　　黑须倒卷帘方：用大马蜞二三十条，竹筒装之，夜置露处受气，饿过七日，以鸡冠血磨京墨与食过四五次，复阴干，将猪胫骨打断，放蜞入内，仍合定铁线缠住盐泥涂之，干时，放地上火煅，五寸香二次；退开三寸火，又五寸香三次；再退远火，又五寸香。取出为末，将猪胆皮包指承末搽须，梢即倒上也。[54p]

    Teeth Cleaning Black Mustache Preparation: Eight taels of coarse rice cakes and three taels of salt flower; use ten jin of fresh wild chrysanthemum roots to extract juice. Combine all in a kettle and boil down until dry. Cover with an iron lid, seal with salt clay, and calcine it red. Grind to a powder and use three times daily. After finishing, drink ginger tea, starting from the eyebrows, for one month until it turns all black.

    Mustache Dyeing Method: One large turtle, starved for a day or two, fed with rice and bones cooked over fire for three to five months. At night, place it in a lacquered box and put a bamboo piece over the mouth to allow for ventilation, with a lamp outside. The box will get hot, causing the turtle to urinate; if urgent, use sesame oil smoke to stimulate its nose, which will also result in urination. First, stir fivefold galls with vinegar until it becomes like glue; if you obtain a small jar of urine, add half a jar of fivefold vinegar, and boil briefly in a ceramic pot until it stops. Store it in a cow horn container, and use a fresh brush to lightly dip and apply to the mustache, preferably using black powder.

    Black Mustache Rolling Method: Use twenty to thirty large horse flies, place them in a bamboo tube, and leave it exposed to dew at night for fresh air. Starve them for seven days, then grind chicken comb blood with ink and add food four to five times more. Dry them again in the dark, break pig tibia bones, place the flies inside, and tightly bundle with iron wire, coating with salt clay. When dry, place over fire and calcine, repeating for five inch incense twice; withdraw three inches of fire, then five inch incense three times; again, pull away further, using five inch incense once more. Take out the powder, wrap it in pig bile skin, and apply to the mustache; it immediately rolls up.[54p]

    　　繁缕为虀，久久食之，能乌髭发。 【《圣惠方》】
    　　疖疮疤上，不生髭发：先以竹刀刮损，以莴苣子拗猢狲姜末，频擦之。 【《摘元方》】
    　　须发拔白换黑：七月七日，取百合熟捣，用新瓷瓶盛之，密封挂门上，阴干百日。每拔去白者掺之，即生黑者也。【《便民图纂》】
    　　令发易长：取东行枣根三尺，横安甑上蒸之，两头汁出，收取敷发，即易长。 【《圣惠方》，下同】
    　　发槁不泽：木瓜浸油梳头。

    　　捻须令黑：酸石榴结成时，就东南枝上拣大者一个，顶上开一孔，内水银半两于中，原皮封之，麻扎紧，牛屎封获，待经霜摘下，倾出壳内水，以鱼鳔笼指蘸水捻须，久久自黑。【《普济方》】[55p]

    • For a long time, eating finely chopped onions can darken one's beard and hair.

    • On abscessed scars, hair does not grow: first scrape with a bamboo knife, then rub with a mixture of lettuce seeds and minced ginger repeatedly.

    • To change white hair to black: on the seventh day of the seventh month, take a ripe lily bulb, pound it, store it in a new ceramic bottle, seal it tightly, and hang it on the door to dry for a hundred days. Each time white hair is plucked, mix it with this and it will grow black.

    • To promote hair growth: take a three-foot-long root from an eastern jujube tree, steam it horizontally in a steamer until juice comes out from both ends, then collect the juice and apply it to the hair to promote growth.

    • For dry, lifeless hair: soak papaya in oil and then comb it.

    • To make whiskers black: when sour pomegranates are in season, select a large one from the southeast branch, make a hole on top, fill it with half a tael of mercury, seal it with the original skin, tie it tightly with hemp, and seal with cow dung. Wait for frost to harvest and pour out the mercury. Dip a fish bladder in the water inside and use it to color the whiskers black over time.[55p]

    　　揩齿乌须：胡桃仁烧过、贝母各等分为散，日日用之揩牙。 【《圣惠方》】
    　　乌须发方：青胡桃三枚，和皮捣细，人乳汁三盏，于银石器内调匀，搽三五次。 【《总录》】
    　　染须发：胡桃根皮一秤，旱莲草十斤，切，以瓮器盛之，入水五斗，浸一月，去滓，熬至五斤，入芸薹子油一斗，慢火煎取五升，收之。凡用先以炭灰汁洗，用油涂之外，以牛柿叶包住，绢裹一夜洗去，用七日即黑也。【《圣济总录》】
    　　大风发脱：毗梨勒烧灰，频擦有效。 【《圣惠方》，下同】
    　　令发不落：榧子三个，胡桃二个，侧柏叶一两，捣浸雪水梳头，发永不落且润也。
    　　发落不生：桐叶一把，麻子仁三升，米泔煮五六沸，去滓，日日洗之则长。 【《肘后方》】
    　　发落不生：合欢木灰二合，墙衣五合，铁精一合，水萍末二合，研匀，生油调涂，一夜一次。【《普济方》】[56p]

    • To cleanse teeth and darken hair: Equal parts roasted walnut kernels and fritillaria, used daily for brushing teeth.
    • For darkening hair: Three green walnuts, ground with the husk, mixed with three cups of human milk, blended in a silver or stone vessel, applied three to five times.
    • For dyeing hair: One pound of walnut root bark, ten jin of drought lotus grass, cut into pieces and soaked in five dou of water in a jar for one month, strained and boiled down to five jin, mixed with one dou of rapeseed oil, simmered to obtain five sheng, then collected. Before use, wash with ash water, apply oil, wrap with cow persimmon leaves, cover with silk overnight, and wash off; within seven days, it will turn black.
    • For hair loss due to strong wind: Burnt ash of piri-le-le, frequently applied is effective.
    • To prevent hair loss: Three nuts from the Torreya tree, two walnuts, and one tael of Chinese arborvitae leaves, crushed and soaked in snow water for combing, prevents hair from falling and keeps it moisturized.
    • For hair loss and no regrowth: A handful of catalpa leaves, three sheng of sesame seeds, boiled in rice wash until it bubbles five to six times, strained, and washed daily for growth.
    • For hair loss and no regrowth: Two he of mimosa wood ash, five he of wall moss, one he of iron essence, and two he of water plant powder, ground together, mixed with raw oil for application once a night.[56p]

    　　头上软疖，令发不生：用抱出鸡卵壳烧存性，研末，入经粉少许，清油调敷。 【《危氏方》】
    　　发白染黑：经霜桐叶及子，多收捣碎，以甑蒸之，生布绞汁，沐头。 【《普济方》】
    　　拔白生黑：婆罗勒即婆罗得也，十颗去皮，取汁，熊脂二两，白马鬐膏炼过一两，生姜炒一两，母丁香半两，为末，和煎，每拔白点之，揩令入肉，即生黑者。【《近效方》 】
    　　染黑须发：桦皮一斤包侧柏一枝，烧烟熏香油碗内，成烟，以手抹在须发上，即黑也。【《多能鄙事》】
    　　发鬓堕落：桑白皮銼二升，以水淹浸，煮五六沸，去滓频频洗沐，自不落也。 【《圣惠方》，下同】
    　　发槁不泽：桑根白皮、柏叶各一片，煎汁沐之即润，神效。
    　　鳖脂主治除白发，除日拔白发，取鳖脂涂孔中即不生。欲再生者，白犬乳汁涂之。 【藏器】[57p]

    1. For soft sores on the scalp that prevent hair from growing: Take the shell of a chicken egg, burn it to preserve its essence, grind it into a powder, mix a small amount with medicinal powder, and apply it with clear oil.

    2. To dye white hair black: Collect frost-coated leaves and seeds of the Paulownia tree, crush them, steam them in a bamboo steamer, extract the juice, and wash the hair with it.

    3. To pull white hair and grow black: Use ten peeled basil seeds to extract the juice, two taels of bear fat, one tael of processed white horse hair fat, one tael of stir-fried ginger, and half a tael of mother clove; grind into powder, mix and boil, and apply to the white spots, rubbing it in so that it turns black.

    4. To dye hair black: Take one pound of birch bark and wrap it around a branch of cypress; burn it to produce smoke, and use your hand to apply the smoke to the hair, which will then turn black.

    5. To prevent hair loss: Take two sheng of white mulberry bark, soak it in water, boil it until it bubbles five or six times, then rinse often, and the hair will not fall out.

    6. For dry, non-lustrous hair: Boil a piece of white mulberry root and a piece of cypress leaf to extract the juice and wash with it for a moisturizing effect.

    7. Bile extract can treat white hair; to prevent white hair from appearing due to plucking, apply bile extract to the area, and it will not grow back. For regrowth, apply the milk of a white dog.[57p]

    　　黑发：于七月七日夜，取萤火虫二七枚，捻发自黑也。 【《便民图纂方》】
    　　乌须黑发如神：旱莲草十六斤，六月下半月、七月上半月采取，不许水洗，扭干取汁，对日晒过五日，不住手搅，午时加入真生姜汁，同好蜜各一斤相和，如前晒搅至数日，似稀糖成膏，磁罐收贮，每日空心好酒一锺，药一匙调服，午后又一服，至二十一日，将白者摘去，即生黑者。名旱莲膏。【《医鉴》】
    　　乌须发方：取大水蛭二个，放磁碗中，饿七日，取乌骨雄鸡血，以松烟墨浓磨汁，倾入猪尿胞内，任水蛭吮饱，将针刺蛭，流出血汁，涂，须发留根二分，其汁浸渍入肉，须发一年茂黑且柔软，极妙不过。　　又方：用大水蛭七枚为末，汞一两，以银三两，作小盒盛之，用蚯蚓泥固济，半指厚深，埋马粪中四十九日，取出化为黑油，以鱼脬笼指，每蘸少许捻须上，其油自然倒行，至根变为黑色也。【《普济方》】[58p]

    Black Hair: On the night of the seventh day of the seventh month, take twenty to thirty fireflies and crush them into your hair to achieve blackness. [From “Convenient Remedies Compilation”]

    Black Hair with Dark Beards: Take sixteen pounds of water lily, harvested in the latter half of June and the first half of July. Do not wash it with water. Twist it dry to extract its juice, and sun-dry it for five days without stopping stirring. At noon, add one pound of fresh ginger juice and one pound of honey, mixing as before, and sun-dry while stirring for several days until it resembles syrupy paste. Store it in a clay jar. Take a spoonful of this medicine with one cup of good liquor on an empty stomach daily; take another dose in the afternoon. After twenty-one days, remove the white portions, leaving the black. This is known as water lily paste. [From “Medical Reference”]

    Formula for Dark Hair: Take two large leeches, place them in a clay bowl, and starve them for seven days. Take the blood of a black-boned rooster, mix it with dense soot from pine smoke, and pour into a pig's bladder, allowing the leeches to suck until they are full. Prick the leeches to draw out their juice, applying it, leaving two centimeters of hair roots. Let the juice seep into the flesh; the hair will become lush, black, and soft within a year, remarkably effective. Another formula: Use seven leeches ground into powder, one ounce of mercury, and three ounces of silver, placed in a small box packed with earth from an earthworm’s habitat, about half a finger thick, buried in horse manure for forty-nine days. After removal, it transforms into black oil. Use a fish bladder to dip a little oil and apply it to the hair; the oil will naturally flow down to the roots, turning them black. [From “Universal Solutions”][58p]

    　　染乌发须：用针砂八两，米酢浸五日，炒略红色，研末，五倍子、百药煎、没石子各二两，诃黎勒皮三两，研包，先以皂荚水洗髭须，用米酢打荞麦面糊和针砂末敷上，荷叶包过一夜，次日取去，以荞麦面糊和四味敷之，一日洗去，即黑。【《圣济总录》】
    　　五倍子一斤研末，铜锅炒之，勿令成块，如有烟起，即提下搅之，从容火上慢炒，直待色黑为度。以湿青布包扎，足踏成饼，收贮听用。每用时，以皂角水洗净须发，用五倍子一两，红铜末酒炒一钱六分，生白矾六分，诃子肉四分，没石子四分，硇砂一分为末，乌梅、酸榴皮煎汤，调匀，碗盛，重汤煮四五十沸，待如饴状，以眉掠刷于须发上，一时洗去，再上，包住，次日洗去，以核桃油润之，半月一染，甚妙。[59p]

    To dye hair black, use eight taels of needle sand, soak in rice vinegar for five days, stir-fry until slightly red, and grind to a powder. Combine with two taels each of gallnut, mixed herbal decoction, and stone powder, plus three taels of myrobalan skin, and grind together. First, wash the beard with soap pod water, then apply a mixture of rice vinegar and buckwheat flour paste with the needle sand powder. Wrap with lotus leaves overnight, then remove it the next day, applying another mixture of buckwheat flour and the four ingredients. Wash off after one day, and it will turn black.

    To prepare the gallnut, grind one catty into a powder and stir-fry in a copper pot without letting it clump. If smoke arises, lift it and stir, slowly frying over a gentle fire until it turns black. Wrap in damp green cloth, press into cakes, and store for use. When needed, wash the hair with soap pod water, then mix one tael of gallnut powder with one and a half maces of red copper powder and six cents of alum, four cents each of myrobalan fruit and stone powder, and one cent of nitre sand into a fine powder. Use the decoction of black plum and sour pomegranate peel, mix well, and cook for about forty to fifty boils until it becomes syrupy. Use a brush to apply to the hair, wash it off after a while, then reapply, covering it up. The next day, wash it off and moisturize with walnut oil. Dye every half month for excellent results.[59p]

    　　眉毛不生：乌麻花阴干为末，乌麻油渍，日涂之。 【《外台秘要》】

    　　　　导引

    　　《延寿书》曰：发多梳则明目去风，故道家晨梳常以百二十为数。　　《类聚》曰：发是血之余，一日一次梳。
    　　　　医案

    　　仲景见侍中王仲宣时年二十余，谓曰：君有病，四十当眉落，眉落半年而死，令服五石汤可免。仲宣嫌其言忤，受汤勿服。居三日，见仲宣谓曰：服汤否？仲宣曰：已服。仲景曰：色候固非服汤之诊，君何轻命也？仲宣犹不信。后二十年，果眉落，后一百八十七日而死，终如其言。
    　　《丹溪心法》曰：胡氏年十七八岁，发脱不留一茎，饮食起居如常，脉微弦而濇，轻重皆同。予曰：此厚味成熟，湿痰在膈间，又日多吃梅，酸味收湿热之痰，随上升之气至于头，蒸熏发根之血，渐成枯槁，遂一时尽脱。遂处以补血升散之药，用防风通圣散去芒硝，惟大黄三度酒炒，兼以四物汤酒制合，和作小剂煎，以灰汤入水频与之，两月余。后诊其脉，湿热渐解，停药淡味调养。又二年，发长如初而愈。
    [62p]

    Guidance

    The "Book of Longevity" states: "Combing the hair often brightens the eyes and wards off wind." Hence, Daoists comb their hair in the morning, typically a hundred and twenty times. The "Compendium" states: "Hair is the surplus of blood; combing once a day."

    Medical Case

    Zhongjing saw the attendant Wang Zhongxuan, who was over twenty years old, and said: "You have a sickness. At forty, your eyebrows will fall, and you will die six months after that." He instructed him to take the Wushi Decoction to avoid this. Zhongxuan disliked his words and took the decoction but did not consume it. Three days later, Zhongjing asked him: "Did you take the decoction?" Zhongxuan replied: "I have taken it." Zhongjing said: "The complexion is not indicative of taking the decoction; why do you take your life lightly?" Zhongxuan still did not believe him. Twenty years later, his eyebrows indeed fell out, and one hundred eighty-seven days after that, he died, thus fulfilling Zhongjing's words.

    The "Danxi Heart Method" states: "A youth named Hu, aged seventeen or eighteen, lost all his hair without leaving a single strand. His diet and daily routines were normal, his pulse was weak and taut yet equal in strength. I said: 'This is due to excessive flavors leading to phlegm-damp in the diaphragm. Additionally, eating too many plums will sour and collect the damp-heat phlegm, which rises to the head, steaming the blood at the hair roots, gradually leading to dryness and eventual hair loss.' I then prescribed blood-tonifying and dispersing herbs, using Fangfeng Tongsheng Powder without the Mangxiao, and only Da Huang stir-fried three times with wine, combined with Siwu Decoction prepared with wine to make a small dose. I frequently administered this with gray decoction in water for over two months. Upon re-evaluation of his pulse, the damp-heat was gradually resolved, and I halted the medicine, adjusting with mild nourishment. Two years later, his hair grew back to its original state and he recovered.[62p]
